<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">dŭk</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/dʌk/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/ducken#Middle_English" title="ducken">ducken</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/duken#Middle_English" title="duken">duken</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/w/index.php?title=douken&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="douken (page does not exist)">douken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to duck, plunge under water, submerge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Old_English/ducan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Old English/ducan (page does not exist)">*dūcan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dip, dive, duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/d%C5%ABkan" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/dūkan">*dūkan</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/d%C5%ABkan%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/dūkaną">*dūkaną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dip, dive, bend down, stoop, duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/d%CA%B0ewb-" class="mw-redirect" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dʰewb-">*dʰewb-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deep, hollow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/d%C5%ABban%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/dūbaną">*dūbaną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Verb"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">duck</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en s-verb-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducks#English" title="ducks">ducks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ing-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducking#English" title="ducking">ducking</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en ed-form-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducked#English" title="ducked">ducked</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To quickly <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/lower#English" title="lower">lower</a> the head or body, often in order to prevent it from being struck by something.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Duck</b>! There's a branch falling off the tree!</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To quickly lower (the head or body), often in order to prevent it from being struck by something.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <span class="None" lang="und"><b>1729</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Swift" class="extiw" title="w:Jonathan Swift">Jonathan Swift</a>, <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Works_of_the_Rev._Jonathan_Swift/Volume_8/To_Dr._Delany_on_the_Libels_Written_Against_Him" class="extiw" title="s:The Works of the Rev. Jonathan Swift/Volume 8/To Dr. Delany on the Libels Written Against Him">To Dr. Delany on the Libels Written Against Him</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">As some raw youth in country bred,<br>To arms by thirst of honour led,<br>When at a skirmish first he hears<br>The bullets whistling round his ears,<br>Will <b>duck</b> his head aside</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1989</b></span>, Grant Naylor, <cite>Red Dwarf: Infinity Welcomes Careful Drivers</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Rimmer <b>ducked</b> his body low into his chair, so just his head remained above the table top, and peered past the backs of the examinees in front of him, waiting for the adjudicator to make his move.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To lower (something) into water; to thrust or plunge under liquid and suddenly withdraw.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1742</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Fielding" class="extiw" title="w:Henry Fielding">Henry Fielding</a>, “A Scene of Roasting Very Nicely Adapted to the Present Taste and Times”, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Andrews" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Andrews">The History of the Adventures of Joseph Andrews, and of His Friend Mr. Abraham Adams.<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written in Imitation of the Manner of Cervantes, Author of Don Quixote. <li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> To go under the surface of water and immediately reappear; to plunge one's head into water or other liquid.

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">duck</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducks#English" title="ducks">ducks</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/caving#Noun" title="caving">caving</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A cave passage containing water with low, or no, airspace.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Etymology 2"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/doke#Middle_English" title="doke">doke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/ducke#Middle_English" title="ducke">ducke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/dukke#Middle_English" title="dukke">dukke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/dokke#Middle_English" title="dokke">dokke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/w/index.php?title=douke&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="douke (page does not exist)">douke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/duke#Middle_English" title="duke">duke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/duce#Old_English" title="duce">duce</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/duce#Old_English" title="duce">dūce</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dipper, diver, ducker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Old_English/ducan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Old English/ducan (page does not exist)">*dūcan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dip, dive, duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/d%C5%ABkan" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/dūkan">*dūkan</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/d%C5%ABkan%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/dūkaną">*dūkaną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dive, bend down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See verb above.

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducke#English" title="ducke">ducke</a></span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">duck</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducks#English" title="ducks">ducks</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink">duck</strong></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>An aquatic <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/bird#English" title="bird">bird</a> of the family <span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Anatidae#Translingual" title="Anatidae">Anatidae</a></span>, having a flat <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/bill#English" title="bill">bill</a> and <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/webbed#English" title="webbed">webbed</a> feet.</li>
<li><i>Specifically</i>, an adult female duck; <i>contrasted with</i> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/drake#English" title="drake">drake</a> <i>and with</i> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/duckling#English" title="duckling">duckling</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> The flesh of a duck used as food.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cricket#English" title="cricket">cricket</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/batsman#English" title="batsman">batsman</a>'s score of <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/zero#English" title="zero">zero</a> after getting out. (short for duck's egg, since the digit "0" is round like an egg.)</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/playing_card#English" title="playing card">playing card</a> with the rank of two.</li>
<li>A building <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/intentionally#English" title="intentionally">intentionally</a> constructed in the shape of an <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/everyday#English" title="everyday">everyday</a> object to which it is related.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><i>A luncheonette in the shape of a coffee cup is particularly conspicuous, as is intended of an architectural <b>duck</b> or folly.</i></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> February 21, Cynthia Blair, “It Happened on Long Island: 1988—Suffolk County Adopts the Big Duck”, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newsday" class="extiw" title="w:Newsday">Newsday</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">The Big Duck has influenced the world of architecture; any building that is shaped like its product is called a ‘<b>duck</b>’.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/marble#English" title="marble">marble</a> to be <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/shoot#English" title="shoot">shot</a> at with another marble (the <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/shooter#English" title="shooter">shooter</a>) in children's games.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cairn#English" title="cairn">cairn</a> used to mark a trail.</li>
<li>One of the weights used to hold a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/spline#English" title="spline">spline</a> in place for the purpose of drawing a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/curve#English" title="curve">curve</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/finance#Noun" title="finance">finance</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/lame_duck#English" title="lame duck">lame duck</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who cannot fulfil their contracts</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/medicine#English" title="medicine">medicine</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A long-necked <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/medical#English" title="medical">medical</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/urinal#English" title="urinal">urinal</a> for men; a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/bed_urinal#English" title="bed urinal">bed urinal</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/faggot#English" title="faggot">faggot</a>; a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/meatball#English" title="meatball">meatball</a> made from <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/offal#English" title="offal">offal</a>.</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/LGBT#English" title="LGBT">LGBT</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prison#English" title="prison">prison</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/slang#English" title="slang">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bitch#English" title="bitch">bitch</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/man#English" title="man">man</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/force#English" title="force">forced</a> or <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/coerce#English" title="coerce">coerced</a> into a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/homosexual#English" title="homosexual">homosexual</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/relationship#English" title="relationship">relationship</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/especially#English" title="especially">especially</a> in <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prison#English" title="prison">prison</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b> April 19, Michael Rathbone, “Tell Someone”, in <cite>Gay Community News</cite>, page 4:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">The more passive males are subjected to physical violence. I was subjected to being what they call a punk or a <b>duck</b>, which is someone else's power trip, that's all.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Etymology 3"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/doek#Dutch" title="doek">doek</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/w/index.php?title=doeck&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="doeck (page does not exist)">doeck</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/doec#Middle_Dutch" title="doec">doec</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">linen cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Old_Dutch/doc&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Old Dutch/doc (page does not exist)">*dōc</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/d%C5%8Dk" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/dōk">*dōk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/d%C5%8Dkaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/dōkaz">*dōkaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth, rag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dw%C5%8Dg-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dwōg- (page does not exist)">*dwōg-</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dw%C5%8Dk-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dwōk- (page does not exist)">*dwōk-</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Tuch#German" title="Tuch">Tuch</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/duk#Swedish" title="duk">duk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth, canvas</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/d%C3%BAkur#Icelandic" title="dúkur">dúkur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloth, fabric</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/doek#English" title="doek">doek</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/dook#English" title="dook">dook</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/doock#English" title="doock">doock</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Scotland</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">duck</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducks#English" title="ducks">ducks</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_fabric" data-senseid="fabric"> A tightly-woven cotton <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/fabric#English" title="fabric">fabric</a> used as <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/sailcloth#English" title="sailcloth">sailcloth</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1912</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Katherine_Mansfield" class="extiw" title="w:Katherine Mansfield">Katherine Mansfield</a>, “The Woman At The Store”, in <cite>Selected Short Stories</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">He was dressed in a Jaeger vest—a pair of blue <b>duck</b> trousers, fastened round the waist with a plaited leather belt.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/trousers#English" title="trousers">Trousers</a> made of such material.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1918</b></span> March, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rebecca_West" class="extiw" title="w:Rebecca West">Rebecca West</a> [pseudonym; Cicily Isabel Fairfield], chapter III, in <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Return_of_the_Soldier" class="extiw" title="w:The Return of the Soldier">The Return of the Soldier</a></cite>, 1st US edition, New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Century_Company" class="extiw" title="w:The Century Company">The Century Co.</a>, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/title/222017629">→OCLC</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/returnofsoldier00west2/page/67/mode/1up">pages <span class="None" lang="und">67–68</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">And they would go up and find old Allington, in white <b>ducks</b>, standing in the fringe of long grasses and cow-parsley on the other edge of the island, looking to his poultry or his rabbits.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1954</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doris_Lessing" class="extiw" title="w:Doris Lessing">Doris Lessing</a>, <cite>A Proper Marriage</cite>, HarperPerennial, published <span class="None" lang="und">1995</span>, page <span class="None" lang="und">74</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">A native servant emerged, anonymous in his white <b>ducks</b> and red fez, to say My Player was wanted on the telephone.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Etymology 4"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Potteries_dialect" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Potteries dialect">Potteries dialect</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Black_Country_Accent" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Black Country Accent">Black Country dialect</a> and dialects of the former territory of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mercia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mercia">Mercia</a> (central England). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/dukke#Danish" title="dukke">dukke</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">doll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/docka#Swedish" title="docka">docka</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baby; doll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/doxy#English" title="doxy">doxy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweetheart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=duck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">duck</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ducks#English" title="ducks">ducks</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"><span class="Latn" lang="en">A term of <a href="/wiki/endearment#English" title="endearment">endearment</a></span></span>; <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pet#English" title="pet">pet</a>; <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/darling#English" title="darling">darling</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1599</b> (date written), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_V_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Henry V (play)">The Life of Henry the Fift</a>”, in <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp;
